**A**

**A, a 1.**(first letter of the alphabet) **अ** *m.,***2.**(as a symbol, used to denote or indicate anyone or

anything arbitrarily or conveniently so designated, esp. as the first in order or class, *e.g.*, the front of the leaf in a book) **क** *m.* (in case of distinction being required between small and capital letters—a क, A का),**3.**(not *cap.*) *Alg.* **क** *m.*

**A, a** *adj.* **1.**(first in order or class, *e.g.*company A,quire a) **क, प्रथम,**

**A1.** *adj.* **सर्वप्रथम, वरेण्य, अ१**

**2.**(having the form of capital A, *e.g.*, an A tent) **प्रउग, प्रउगाकार** (of the form of aप्रउग-चिति. See Journal of Vedic Studies Vol. I pp. 127-8)

**a** *prep.* (on, in, at) **अधि-** (ashore अधिवेलम्), **पर**  
**a-** (negative prefix) **अ-, निर्-**

**परिनिपातन**(परि entirely, नि down, पातन felling),**3.**(to demolish, throw or pull down),**अवासन** (अव down, असन throwing), **नीचे गिराना**, **4.**(to put an end to) **अन्त-करण, अन्त करना, समाप्त करना,5.**(to nullify; to make void) **शून्य-करण, शून्यन** (शून्य void),**6.***intr*. (to lessen) **हसन, न्यून होना, कम होना,***trans.* **ह्रासन, ह्रास करना, न्यून करना, कम करना,7.**(to diminish, as a disease) **उपशमन,****8.**(to subside) **प्रशमन, अधोगमन, नीचे उतरना** (the waters of the river aba-

ted नदी का पानी नीचे उतर गया), **9.***Law* **उपसंहरण होना, उपशमन होना, समाप्त होना**

**abstract** *vb.* (to withdraw) **निवर्तन, अपकर्षण, अपनयन** (take away)**, निकालना, पृथक्करण**

(separate)**, वियोजन, विवेचन** (as, to abstract the notion of dimension from that of space), **गूढ-ग्रहण, रहसि-ग्रहण** (to tako secretly)**, कूटग्रहण** (to take dishonestly)**, संक्षेप करना, संक्षिप्ति बनाना** (to summarise)

**abstract** *adj.* **1.**(considered apart from any application to a particular object) **केवल** (occurs in

ऋग्वेद, पाणिनि, etc)**, निरपेक्ष, 2.निगूढ़, दुरूह, दुर्ज्ञेय, अमूर्त, 3.***Math.* (used without reference to a thing) **अमूर्त, 4**.(expressing a property, quality or attribute) **भाववाची** (-इन्),**5.***Logic* **गुणवाचक, गुणवाची** (-इन्),**6.**(general) **सामान्य, अविशेष** (*opp. particular*), **7.**(applied to *pure sciences* as disting from *applied sciences*) **शुद्ध, अव्यावहारिक, 8.***Paint., Sculp***. कल्पित, 9.असंबद्ध, 10.-मात्र, 11.संक्षिप्त**

abundantly

*adv.*

abundant number

(a number as 4 which is less ऊन than the sum योग of its various divisors

1, 2, 2)

गुणोनयोग संख्या  
deficient or defective number

(as 12, which is greater अधिक than the sum of its various divisors 1, 2, 2, 3)

गुणाधिकयोग संख्या, हीन संख्या  
perfect number

(as 6, which is equal सम to the sum of its various divisors 1, 2, 3)

गुणसम-योग संख्या, संपूर्ण संख्या  
imperfect number

(either greater or less असम than the sum of its various divisors)

गुणासमयोग संख्या, असंपूर्ण संख्या

accessories उपसाधन** *n.*  
**accessorium non ducit sed sequitur suum principale** ("That which is the accessory or

incident does not lead, but follows its principal") **गौणः प्रधानमनुसरति, न हि प्रधानो गौणम्। गौण प्रधान का अनुसरण करता है, न कि प्रधानगौण का।**

**accessorium non trahit principale** ("The accessory does not draw the principal." The release

of surety is not the release of his principal,although the release of principal is the release of the surety also) **न**

**गौणः प्रधानं कर्षति । गौण प्रधान को कभी नहीं खींचता।**

**accessorium sequiture principale** (“The accessory follows its principal", where there is no

principal there can be no accessory) **गौणः प्रधानमनुसरति प्रधाने सत्येव गौणः॥ गौण प्रधान का अनुसरण करता है। प्रधान के न होने पर गौणहो ही नहीं सकता।**

**accessorius** *Anat.* **1.उप-पेशी** *f.* (पेशी muscle),**2.= accessory nerve उप-चेता** *f.*  
**accessorius sequitur naturam sui principalis** ("An accessory follows the nature of his

principal")

**गौणः प्रधानस्वभावमनुसरति। गौण अपने प्रधान के स्वभाव का अनुसरण करता है।**

Aleurites moluccana** (Bengal walnut, Belgaun walnut, candle nut, Indian walnut) **सामान्य मलयाक्षोट**

(it is the native of Malay Peninsula and hence our name मलयाक्षोट. We have taken अक्षोट as *Jugulans regia.* Basu however considers *Aleurites moluccana* as the Indian walnut अक्षोट. An alternative name given by Basu is Bengal walnut. Webster also registers Indian walnut for *Aleurites moluccana.* Apparently the word Indian has been used in a wider sense including Malay Peninsula and the East Indies.)
